  // Added assertions to support the proof of minimality

  // Lemma: If 1 <= s' < val, then s' < a + b
  lemma Lemma1(a: int, b: int, val: int, s': int)
    requires 1 <= s' < val
    ensures s' < a + b
  {
    // val <= a + b from earlier assertion
    assert val <= a + b;
    // Since s' < val, transitivity gives s' < a + b
    assert s' < val ==> s' < a + b;
  }

  // Lemma: For any s' < val, we have 2*a <= s' implies a <= s'
  lemma Lemma2(a: int, b: int, val: int, s': int)
    requires 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !(2 * a <= s' && a <= s')
  {
    // If 2*a <= s' then a <= s' trivially, but we need to show impossible
    // Since s' < val and val >= 2*a, s' < 2*a, so 2*a <= s' can't hold
    assert val >= 2 * a;
    assert s' < val ==> s' < 2 * a;
    assert !(2 * a <= s');
  }

  // Lemma: For any s' < val, we have 2*b <= s' implies b <= s'
  lemma Lemma3(a: int, b: int, val: int, s': int)
    requires 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !(2 * b <= s' && b <= s')
  {
    // If 2*b <= s' then b <= s' trivially, but we need to show impossible
    // Since s' < val and val >= 2*b, s' < 2*b, so 2*b <= s' can't hold
    assert val >= 2 * b;
    assert s' < val ==> s' < 2 * b;
    assert !(2 * b <= s');
  }

  method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
    requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
    ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
  {
    var lo := if a < b then a else b;
    var hi := if a < b then b else a;
    var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

    // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
    assert val >= 1;
    assert lo <= hi;

    // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
    if a <= b {
      // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
      assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
      assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
    } else {
      // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
      assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
      assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
    }
    assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

    // Key inequality: val <= a + b
    // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
    // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
    assert val <= a + b;

    // Show minimality: no smaller square works
    forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
      ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
    {
      // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
      assert !(a + b <= s');

      // Use Lemma1 to deduce s' < a + b
      assert Lemma1(a, b, val, s');

      if a <= b {
        // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
        assert 2 * b >= val;
        // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
        // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
        assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
        // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
        // s' < 2*b, so fails
        assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
        // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
        // s' < 2*b, so fails
        assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
        // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
        // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
        assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
      } else {
        // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
        assert 2 * a >= val;
        assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
        assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');

        assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
      }

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;

  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {

    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;

  assert val <= a + b;

      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');
    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{

  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');

      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)

  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val;
    assert b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val;
    assert a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');
    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)

}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

```dafny
  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{

  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  var hi := if a < b then b else a;

  assert lo <= hi;

    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);

// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;

```dafny
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

<DAFNY_CODE>
method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * a <= val || b <= val; // derived from val definition
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s'); // fails because s' < val
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s'); // fails because s' < 2*b
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s'); // fails because s' < 2*b
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s'); // fails because s' < val
    } else {
      assert 2 * b <= val || a <= val; // derived from val definition
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
